The hotel's front desk service is really good. The staff are friendly and welcoming, making you feel extra warm. They were professional and efficient, and check-in and check-out were very quick. msg:I am from Jiangsu, and it is also a guesthouse, which cannot be compared with Yangzhou Guesthouse!
It was my first time to Jiangxi. I went to Shangri-La (a hotel in 2016, with decent maintenance) to see the night view on the first night. I chose Qianhu for the second night because I checked in at night. The greenery after entering the door was very impressive. I checked in late, but the front desk didn't ask and gave me the last room. I was speechless! Because it was in Building 3, I had to walk a long way! I saw several rooms seemed to be renovated along the way, ******, ***************, **, ************* (if it was renovated, shouldn't the rooms nearby be given to guests?) I finally walked to the room, but it turned out to be the last room. It felt like there were no guests on both sides. I thought I had to go to the city tomorrow, so I didn't care! As a result, the balcony of the room was half open, and there was a big bug on the curtain! I was too lazy to go to the front desk to change rooms, so I just took a shower and went to bed!
I took a photo when I went out to the basement the next day (the picture below). It's hard to comment! This is probably the worst guesthouse I've ever stayed in. 5 points, 1.5 points at most (1 point for the greenery). I won't come again next time! It doesn't deserve this title.
